# Text Elements
the force exerted by and engine in a motorcycle acts in the same
direction as the motion Calculate the work done if the engine exerts 
a force or 3400N in a distance of 80m ^qyWp0CTN

Clearly w = fscos ^eVEkqyR4

A man exerts a force of 28N at and angle ot 60 degrees 
to the direction of motion as he pushes a pram
200.0m on a flat path. find work done ^bVEkuDXs

Clearly W=fs*cos ^N424Yg71

W=28(200)*cos(60) = 2800J






 ^e1Os1gZO

force ^fIP2fMLT

displacement ^X9GmXaaH

10 ^56XHejKQ

20 ^Pp2Lc9hg

5 ^a8rMOVSi
